Appellant</span></strong></span></p><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 6.0pt; text-align: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">-Versus-</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">The State </span></strong></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: right; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 9pt;">(In Criminal Appeal No. 9170 of 2015)</span></em></strong></span></p><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: center; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">With</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 6.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">Md. Sharif</span></strong></span></p><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 6.0pt; text-align: center; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">-Versus-</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">The State </span></strong></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: right; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 9pt;">(In Jail Appeal No. 222 of 2015)</span></em></strong></span></p><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: center; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">And</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 6.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Md. Mintu Khan</span></strong></span></p><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 6.0pt; text-align: center; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">-Versus-</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">The State </span></strong></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: right; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 9pt; line-height: 110%;">(In Jail Appeal No. 224 of 2015)</span></em></strong></span></p></td></tr></tbody></table></div><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 112%; tab-stops: right 210.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Evidence Act (I of 1872)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 112%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Section 32(1)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 112%; tab-stops: right 210.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">The declarations were taken by the trial court as if in the words of the victim. Such statements made by the victim prior to his death [around 2-4 hours before his death], cannot be said to be untrue and unauthenticated. Even then, no inconsistent versions regarding dying declarations of the victim are found among the witnesses who provided the victim’s declarations of his attack. Here we find the dying declarations of the victim provided by the said witnesses are consistent and corroborative to each other.   . . . (43)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 112%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Code of Criminal Procedure (V of 1898)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 6.0pt; line-height: 112%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Section 342</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 112%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Evidence Act (I of 1872)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 112%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Section 24</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 112%; tab-stops: right 210.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">On a plain reading of their confessions it is clearly found that they made the confessions involving themselves in the commission of offence. So, there is no doubt that the confessions of the accused are inculpatory in nature. The confessions are so natural and spontaneous that one cannot harbor any doubt about its voluntariness. When a confession is found to be true and voluntary and inculpatory in nature without corrobo-rating evidence a conviction can be imposed upon the maker of the statement.          . . .(60)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Evidence Act (I of 1872)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Section 8</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 110%; tab-stops: right 210.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">In this case the intention of the perpetrators is totally absent. They did not call the victim with a pre-planned manner rather when they saw the victim near the motor garage, one of them took him inside the garage. So, it is a clear case of no evidence as regard to the intention of the perpetrators. But they intended to give him some blue air into his belly through his private soft organ after taking off his trousers is indicating that they made themselves to commit a heinous crime with a teenage victim.    . . .(63)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Penal Code (XLV of 1860)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Section 302</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 110%; tab-stops: right 210.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">In the case in hand it appears from evidence that the death of the victim was caused by blue air pumped into his belly through inflator by the condemned prisoners. Such act of the condemned prisoners proves that they did it with the intention of causing such bodily injury and ultimate result came into death of the victim and as such they cannot escape themselves from such liability as stated above under section 302 of the Penal Code.         . . .(75)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Evidence Act (I of 1872)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Section 45</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 110%; tab-stops: right 210.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">It appears from dissection of autopsy report, prepared by pw-37 that the abdomen of the victim was distended and the anterior abdominal highly congested. The small intestine and whole large intestine was ruptured and gangrenous and the urinary bladder was ruptured and also both lungs were collapsed. Such analysis proved that inside the body of the victim was disrupted by the blue air pumped through the inflator by the condemned prisoners.                                         . . . (76)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Penal Code (XLV of 1860)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Sections 300, 302, 304 and 34</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 110%; tab-stops: right 210.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Where the accused has the guilty intention of causing such injury as is likely to cause death the offence cannot be converted into one under first part of section 304 of the Penal Code, unless it is brought to any of the five exceptions of section 300 of the Penal Code. In the instant case, both the condemned prisoners had guilty intention and common intention to cause bodily injury as is likely to cause death. And therefore, there is no scope to alter the sentence to one under section 304 from 302 of the Penal Code as advanced by the learned Advocates, for the condemned prisoners. Furthermore, the common intention under section 34 of the Penal Code can be established as an inference from the fact of participation in the commission of the offence.     . . . (79)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Code of Criminal Procedure (V of 1898)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 6.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Section 376</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Penal Code (XLV of 1860)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Section 302/34</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 112%; tab-stops: right 210.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">From the evidence of witnesses it is found that the accused persons removed the victim from the place of occurrence to the hospitals soon after incident. It is also evident by pws-25, 33 and 34 that the accused persons were beaten by angry mobs after occurrence meaning that the accused persons did not flea away rather they tried to save the life of the victim when they felt that they committed serious crime on the victim by pumping air into his belly by inflator.</span></strong> <strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">In such a situation, it is a very hard job for the court to determine the quantum of sentence whether it will be capital punishment or imprisonment for life upon the accused persons since they played a role for saving the victim’s life soon after occurrence as evident by the said prosecution witnesses. At the same time it is very important to note that the victim was completely an innocent teenager who had no fault of such dire consequences at the hands of the accused persons. Since the determination of awarding sentence to the accused persons is at the middle point of views, it may turn to impose capital punishment or imprisonment for life and that is why, the advantage of lesser one shall find the accused persons to acquire in the instant case. Moreso, both the accused persons have no significant history of prior criminal activities and their PC and PR [previous conviction and previous records] are found nil in the police report.</span></strong> <strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">It also indicates from the evidence of prosecution witnesses that doctors got confused as to how the treatment was given to the victim when he was taken to the hospitals in Khulna Divisional Head Quarters because it was an exceptional offence committed by the accused persons and the victim died around four hours later on the way to Dhaka. Therefore, we do find an extraneous ground to commute the sentences but we do not find any reason to interfere with conviction recorded under sections 302/34 of the Penal Code.</span></strong> <strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">In the above facts and circumstances of the case, we are of the view that ends of justice will be met if the accused persons are sentenced to one of imprisonment for life instead of awarding them sentences to death with a fine of Tk. 50[fifty] thousand each, in default, to under R.I for 02[two] years.             . . .(85 to 87)</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 112%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">3 DLR 388; 7 BLC 265; 8 BLC 132;</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">12 DLR (WP) Lahore 30 (DB);</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">42 DLR 397;</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Islam Uddin Vs. State, 13 BLC [AD] 81;</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">State Vs. Munir and another, 1 BLC, 345;</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Mufti Abdul Hannan Munshi @ Abul Kalam and another Vs. the State, 2017(1) LNJ (AD)38;</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Rajwant Vs. State of Kerala AIR 1966 SC, 1874;</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Ayub Ali alias Md. Ayub Ali Vs. The State, 1987 BCR [AD] 66; Govt. of Bangladesh Vs. Siddique Ahmed, 31 DLR [AD] [1997] 29;</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Tera mean Vs. Crown, 7 DLR 539;</span></em></strong> <strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">63 DLR 460, 18 BLD 81 and 57 DLR 591 and Nalu Vs. The State, 1 ALR (AD) (2012) 222 ref.</span></em></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; letter-spacing: -0.3pt; font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">Mr. Golam Mohammad Chowdhury with</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Mr.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Md.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Hemayth Uddin and</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; letter-spacing: -0.4pt;">Mr.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; letter-spacing: -0.4pt;"> Md.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; letter-spacing: -0.4pt;"> Akhteruzzaman Talukder, Advs.</span></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: right; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">. . .For the appellant<u> </u></span></strong></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: right; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 9pt; line-height: 110%;">(In Criminal Appeal No. 9051 of 2015)</span></em></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: .5in; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">With</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">Mr. S. M Abdul Mobin with</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">Mr. Mahabub-Ule-Islam</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Mr.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Md.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Muhibullah Tanvir</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Mr.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Md.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Emran Khan and</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Mr.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Md.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Abdus Salam, Advocates</span></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: right; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">. . . For the appellant<u> </u></span></strong></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: right; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 9pt; line-height: 110%;">(In Criminal Appeal No. 9170 of 2015)</span></em></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent: .5in; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">With</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">Mr. Zahirul Haque Zahir, D.A.G with</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Mr.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Md.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> Atiqul Haque [Selim], A.A.G</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">Ms. Bilkis Fatema, A.A.G and</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">Mr. Nizamul Haque Nizam, A.A.G</span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: right; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">. . .For the State<u> </u></span></strong></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: right; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 110%;">(In Jail Appeal No. 222 of 2015 and Jail Appeal No. 224 of 2015)</span></em></span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; text-align: right; line-height: 112%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;"> </span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">Mr. Kazi Md. Sajawar Hossain, Advocate</span></p><p align="right" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: right; text-indent: .5in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><em><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 10pt;">.....[assisted the State informally during CAV of the Death Reference]</span></em></strong></span></p><p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 6.0pt; text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span style="font-size: 11pt;">JUDGMENT</span></strong></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27.35pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><u><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; letter-spacing: -0.4pt;">Jahangir Hossain, J:</span></u></strong> <span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; letter-spacing: -0.4pt;">This Death Reference</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; letter-spacing: -0.2pt;"> No.</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;"> 92 of 2015 is the outcome of judgment and order of conviction and sentence dated <span style="letter-spacing: -0.3pt;">08.11.2015 referred by the learned Metropolitan</span> Sessions Judge [in-charge], Khulna for confirmation of death sentence to condemned prisoners, Md. Sharif Sheikh and Md. Mintu Khan @ Mintu under section 374 of the Code of Criminal Procedure [briefly Cr.P.C].</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">2.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">            </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Challenging the said judgment and order of conviction and sentence condemned prisoners, Md. Sharif Sheikh and Md. Mintu Khan @ Mintu both filed two separate petitions of appeals being numbered as Criminal Appeal Nos. 9051 of 2015 and 9170 of 2015 and also filed two separate Jail Appeal Nos. 222 of 2015 and 224 of 2015 respectively. The aforesaid Death Reference and all criminal appeals have been heard together and are disposed of by this common judgment. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">3.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">            </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">The prosecution case is briefly described as under: </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 27.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">On 04.08.2015 Md. Nurul Alam, the father of the deceased, being informant lodged an FIR with Khulna Police Station against the condemned prisoners and accused Beauty Begum, mother of condemned prisoner Md. Sharif Sheikh, alleging inter alia that his son Rakib Hawlader worked in the motorcycle service centre namely ‘Sharif Motors’ situated at North-East corner of Tutpara graveyard at Khan Jahan Ali Road, Khulna owned by condemned prisoner Sharif who used to give him less wages and often beat him. Due to this reason, Rakib left the job and joined another work place namely ‘Nur Alam Motors’ where he was doing the same task for about 3/4 months. On 03.08.2015 around 04:30 pm when his son reached near the aforesaid place in order to purchase colour paint, condemned prisoner Sharif forcibly took him into his motor garage where condemned prisoner Mintu and accused Beauty Begum were also present. On an inquiry Rakib replied that he left the job because condemned prisoner Sharif did not give him adequate salary. Being enraged condemned prisoner Sharif used abusive words with him who raised his voice on it. </span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">4.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">            </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Thereafter, condemned prisoner Mintu along with accused Beauty Begum held Rakib and laid him down on the floor taking off his trousers and forcibly inserted a high pressure air pump nozzle into his rectum while condemned prisoner Sharif switched on of the inflator. As a result, his son became severely injured and his belly also got abnormally puffed having clotted blood in the rectum and intestines tore apart and lunges burst as air filled the abdomen. They all shut down the shutter of the garage to confirm his death while his son was groaning. Having reached the place on hearing hue and cry surrounding locals came to the spot and rescued him from the garage and instantly took him to local ‘Good Health Clinic’ from where he was referred to Khulna Medical College Hospital as his condition deteriorated. Thereafter, doctor of the KMCH referred him to Dhaka Medical College Hospital for better treatment. At about 09:30 pm on the way to Dhaka from Khulna he died in the ambulance. Having arrived home he [informant] came to know the incident from his wife and locals. The accused persons were confined and beaten by angry mobs on hearing death news of his son and handed them over to the police. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">5.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">            </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Having received the FIR police recorded Khulna Police Station Case No.04 dated 04.08.2015 against the aforesaid accused persons under sections 302/34 of the Penal Code.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">6.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">            </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Police thereafter held inquest report of dead body of the deceased and seized some materials relating to the death of the deceased. During investigation of the case both the condemned prisoners and accused Beauty Begum made confessional statements before the magistrate under section 164 of the Cr.P.C. The investigating officer after completion of investigation submitted police report being charge sheet No. 275 dated 25.08.2015 against the three accused persons including the condemned prisoners under sections 302/34 of the Penal Code, 1860. All the accused persons were put on trial by the learned Metropolitan Sessions Judge [In-charge], Khulna in Metropolitan Sessions Case No. 1161 of 2015. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">7.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">            </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Gravamen of charge against three accused persons was framed on 05.10.2015 under the aforesaid sections, as stated in the charge sheet which was read over and explained to them present on dock to which they pleaded not guilty and claimed to be innocent in the trial. The prosecution in order to prove its case, examined in all 38[thirty eight] out of 40[forty] witnesses cited in the charge sheet while defence did not call any witness in their favour, but put their case by <span style="letter-spacing: -0.3pt;">way of suggestions to the prosecution witnesses.</span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">8.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">            </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">On closure of the prosecution evidence, the accused persons present in dock, were also examined under section 342 of the Cr.P.C wherein the incriminating evidence and confessions brought to their notices and consequence thereof were explained to them. The accused persons present in the dock reiterated their innocence, non-complicity and declined to adduce any evidence in their favour through defence witnesses but they orally narrated before the court that they were compelled to confess by torture and also fearing cross-fire.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">9.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">            </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Considering the evidence and facts and circumstances of the case, learned Metropolitan Sessions Judge found the condemned prisoners guilty of the offence punishable under sections 302/34 of the Penal Code and sentenced them to death while acquitted accused Beauty Begum from the charge levelled against her. Hence, the aforesaid death reference and criminal appeals have been arisen.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">10.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Mr. Md. Atiqul Haque @ Selim along with Mr. Md. Nizamul Haque Nizam and Ms. Bilkis Fatema, learned Assistant Attorney Generals has taken us to the FIR, inquest report, confessional statements, autopsy report, seizure list, seizing articles, testimony of the witnesses and impugned judgment and other connected documents on record wherefrom it transpires that the victim was killed by the condemned prisoners on 03.08.2015 between 04:30 pm and 09:30 pm.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">11.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Having gone through the evidence of all the prosecution witnesses it is found that pw-01 Nurul Alam, father of the victim, is not an eye witness to the occurrence but he heard the incident that accused Sharif forcibly took the victim inside the shop and switched inflator on while accused Mintu pressed inflator’s pipe in the rectum, as a result, victim’s belly got puffed and subsequently he died. Such facts he received from his relatives and locals. The story of ejahar [exhibit-01] lodged by him, has been supported by his subsequent evidence, deposed in court.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">12.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-02 Constable Badrul Alam is a member of rescue party, who saw the beating upon the three persons including a woman and took them to the hospital after rescue them from the angry mobs on 03.08.2015 at 11:30 pm. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">13.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-03 Zahidul Islam is also a hearsay witness who heard the incident from the mother of the victim that Sharif and Mintu gave blue air inside the rectum of the victim and pw-04 Mizan Howlader is an important witness in this case because he heard from the mouth of the accused Sharif that he pumped air inside the belly of the victim. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">14.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-05 Khokon Sheikh and pw-08 Ruksana heard from pw-14 Shahidul, a helper of ‘Nur Alam Motors’ that accused Sharif and Mintu gave blue air through inflator’s pipe in the rectum of the victim but subsequently victim Rakib told pw-05 that Sharif held him and Mintu gave air into the rectum by machine. Pw-10 Rimi, pw-11 Lucky Begum and pw-13 Sujon directly heard from victim Rakib that accused Mintu pressed pipe while Sharif switched on of the inflator machine during the occurrence.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">15.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-06 Constable Maksudul Haque is a formal witness who received the dead body of the victim and took the same to the hospital for autopsy and signed the seizure list of wearing apparels of the victim.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">16.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-07 Md. Zahirul Islam is also a member of rescue party who rescued three persons including a woman from the angry mobs on 03.08.2015 at 23:10 pm and came to know that victim died due to sustaining blue air pumped by inflator machine in the anus and due to late night he could not prepare inquest report but the same was held next morning at 08:00 am [exhibit-02].</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-09 Khadiza, grandmother of the victim, saw the victim feeling unwell in the hospital on 03.08.2015 and she became unconscious and saw him died after regain.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-12 Selina Rahman heard the incident the following day that Rakib was given blue air and the shop of ‘Sharif Motor Garage’ was provided on a rental basis by her father.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-14 Shahidul Sheikh heard that blue air was given inside the rectum of the victim and he signed the seizure list of a navy blue trousers and a color paint pot recovered by police from the house of Rakib. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">20.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-15 Durgapada Bowliah, O.T in-charge of Gazi Medical College Hospital, Khulna, saw the belly of the victim Rakib abnormally puffed and saliva coming out from his nose and mouth on 03.08.2015 at 05:30 pm and victim told him that his one uncle by pressing inflator’s pipe in the rectum pumped blue air in the shop where the victim worked before. They committed the crime by calling him because he was working in another shop after resigning from the earlier one. Anaesthesia doctor told this witness that it was not possible to treat the victim in their hospital, then, they left with victim.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">21.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-16 Md. Nur Alam is a hearsay witness who heard that both the accused Sharif and Mintu gave air into his belly. Having gone to the surgical clinic he found victim Rakib’s belly being puffed and on the way to Dhaka he eventually died. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">22.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-17 Md. Sorowar Hossain is also a hearsay witness who heard that the victim died due to blue air pumped by inflator machine. In his presence police recovered two inflators and a sandal and prepared a seizure list which he signed as witness. He recognized the alamots in court. Pw-18 Kamrul Mollah echoed the same voice as deposed by pw-17.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">23.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-19 Sumon Howlader heard that Sharif and Mintu gave air inside rectum of the victim who felt sick severely and he gave a bag of blood for victim Rakib and he heard at night that Rakib had died.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">24.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-20 Nabil Hasan Fahim in his deposition stated that accused Mintu forcibly took the victim Rakib inside the shop and accused Sharif switched on of the machine. Thereafter, victim Rakib started vomiting while he was standing in front of the shop. He had seen Rakib vomiting on his own eyes.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">25.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-21 Md. Selim Sheikh stated in his examination-in-chief that accused Sharif and Mintu both have pumped blue air inside the rectum of the victim by pressing inflator machine. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">26.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-22 Md. Zahirul Islam said, police seized two inflator machines and a sandal of Rakib in his presence and signed the seizure list and also identified the sandal in court. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">27.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-23 Md. Robiul Islam Howlader testified that Rakib came to his shop and left after buying colour paint and he could see vomiting in front of the shop and he heard from pw-20 that accused Mintu took the victim inside the shop and pressed the inflator’s pipe in the rectum of the victim while Sharif switched on of the inflator and he heard at night that Rakib had died. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">The evidence of Pw-24 Tahmina Akhter is that she saw the belly of the victim hard and abnormally puffed when Rakib was taken to clinic.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; line-height: 110%;">29.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-25 Sheikh Asaduzzaman Jalal is a seizure list witness who signed the seizure list of shirt, trousers and shawl of victim Rakib.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-26 Sheikh Mosharaf Hossain, staff nurse of Khulna Sadar Hospital, saw a boy brought by some persons in the hospital on 03.08.2015 in the afternoon and he heard that some youths pumped air in the rectum by making fun. Doctor suggested to take him to 250 beds’ hospital as his condition seemed to be fatal. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">31.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-27 Md. Zafor Kalifa, a staff nurse of Khulna Sadar Hospital, Pw-30 Constable Khusrul Alam and Pw-36 Provash Chandra Golder, an administrative officer of ‘Good Health Clinic’, Khulna have been tendered by the prosecution and defence declined to cross-examine them.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">32.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-28 S.I Md. Alam verified the address of accused Sharif and Beauty and found correct.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">33.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-29 Constable Nurul Islam testified that he was on patrol duty under leadership of S.I Zahirul Islam on 03.08.2015 and rescued accused Sharif, Mintu and Beauty Begum from the hands of angry people from Tutpara Tank Road after getting message at 23:30 hours and heard that the boy named Rakib was killed by gas.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">34.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-31 Sukumar Biswas, officer-in-charge, Khulna Police Station is a formal witness who filled up the FIR form, marked as exhibit-12.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">35.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-32 S.I Taposh Kumar is also a formal witness who received the autopsy report [exhibit-13] of deceased Rakib from Khulna Medical College Hospital.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">36.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-33 Aysha Akhter Mousumi, Metropolitan Magistrate, Khulna recorded confession of accused Beauty Begum on 07.08.2015 under section 164 of the Cr.P.C. The accused signed the confessional statement, marked as exhibit-14 wherein she put her signatures.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">37.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-34 Md. Faruk Iqbal, Metropolitan Magistrate, Khulna recorded the confessional statements of accused Sharif and Mintu when they were produced before him on 11.08.2015 and 12.08.2015 respectively. Before recording their confessions he alerted both of them that he would not send them to the police custody if they do not confess and he also gave them sufficient reflection time. Accused Sharif signed the confessional statement, marked as exhibit-15 and he also put nine signatures thereon. Accused Mintu Khan signed his confessional statement, marked as exhibit-16 wherein this witness put nine signatures. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">38.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-35 Dr. Subrata Kumar Mondal, Assistant Registrar of Khulna Medical College Hospital, stated that Rakib [15] was admitted to their hospital on 03.08.2015. He placed the document, marked as exhibit-17.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">39.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">Pw-37 Dr. Mohammad Wahid Mahmud rendered autopsy report after examining the dead body of the victim on 04.08.2015. The autopsy report contains the following injuries,</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level7 lfo1; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">1.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">      </span></span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">Bruise was present on both wrists joint.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level7 lfo1; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">2.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">      </span></span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">Bruise was present on both ankles joint.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; mso-list: l0 level7 lfo1; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 6.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">3.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">      </span></span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt;">Abrasion was present on dorsum of the right foot.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level7 lfo1; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt .5in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">4.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">      </span></span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Clotted blood on anus.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: .25in; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Dissection: </span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">The abdomen was distended. The anterior abdominal highly congested. Ante-mortem clotted blood was present on the peritoneal cavity. The small intestine and whole large intestine was ruptured and gangrenous. The urinary bladder was ruptured. Both lungs were collapsed.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: .25in; line-height: 110%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Opinion:</span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;"> The cause of death was due to haemorrhage as shock as a result of above mentioned injury which was ante-mortem and homicidal in nature.   </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">40.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">Pw-38 S.I Kazi Mustaque Ahmed submitted police report [charge sheet No. 275 dated 25.08.2015] as investigator after completing investigation against the three accused persons under sections 302/34 read with section 201 of the Penal Code.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">41.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">In this case none of the prosecution witnesses saw the occurrence directly except pw-20 whose evidence reveals that accused Mintu grappled the victim inside the shop and pumped air inside his anus by inflator pipe while Sharif switched it on and this witness also saw the victim vomiting which was supported by pw-16 that he found sign of vomiting near his shop. Prior to the death, the victim made dying declarations before pws. 03, 05, 10, 11, 13 and 15 that due to resigning from the job of ‘Sharif motors’, accused Sharif pumped air inside his rectum with the help of accused Mintu by inflator on the day of occurrence. This version of evidence has also been corroborated by the extra judicial confession of accused as disclosed by pw-04 in his evidence. In this case dying declaration made by the deceased prior to his death was not recorded by a magistrate or by any other way but it was made orally to the witnesses. Such declaration is admissible even if it were made orally [3 DLR 388, 7 BLC 265 and 8 BLC 132]. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">42.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">A dying declaration is a valuable piece of evidence if it is from suspicion and believed to be true. If a dying declaration is found to be true and genuine, it can be by itself form a satisfactory basis for conviction [12 DLR (WP)Lahore 30 (DB)]. Dying declaration may not be natural if it is recorded by a person with the help of interested persons of the maker. Rather it could be quite natural and true statement when the victim utters orally and instantly the cause of his injuries to the neutral persons who provide version of the victim before the court on oath having is being tested. The court is to see whether the victim had the physical capability of making such a declaration, whether witnesses who had heard the deceased making such statements heard it correctly. Whether the reproduced names of assailants correctly and whether the maker of the declaration had an opportunity to recognise the assailants [42 DLR 397]. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 110%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">43.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 110%;">In the present case dying declarations of the victim have been stated by pws 03, 05, 10, 11, 13 and 15 such as Pw-3 in his deposition said,-</span> </span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-ansi-language: EN;">‘</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;">l¡¢Lh h­®m, j¡j¡<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>Bj¡­®L nl£g, ¢j¾V¥ Hhw ¢hE¢V d­®l f¡R¡</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;"> ®cuz</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-ansi-language: EN;">’ </span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-bidi-font-family: Vrinda; mso-ansi-language: EN;">Pw-13 stated in his examination-in-chief,</span> <span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; mso-ansi-language: EN;">‘</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 110%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;">¢L q­®u­®R<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>S¡e­®a Q¡C­®m ®p<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>h­®m, j¡j¡ nl£g j¡j¡ Bj¡l f¡R¡u<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>q¡Ju¡ ¢c®­u­®Rz a¡l p¡®­b ¢hE¢V, ¢j¾V</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt;
