mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiNormal; mso-ansi-language: EN;">¢</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;">j®­m N¤X Eq~m<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>q¡pf¡a¡®­m ¢e®­u k¡u H¢V ®lLXÑ q®­u®­Rz........ HL S¡uN¡u ®mM¡ B­R, SeNe nl£g®­L j¡l¢fV L®­lz</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; mso-ansi-language: EN;">’ </span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; mso-bidi-font-family: Vrinda; mso-ansi-language: EN;">Pw-34 in cross-examination said,-</span> <span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; mso-ansi-language: EN;">‘</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;">Bp¡j£®­L NZ ®d¡m¡C ®</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiNormal; mso-ansi-language: EN;">cJu¡</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;"> q®­u¢Rm ö­®e¢Rz </span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-ansi-language: EN;">........</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;">NZ ¢fV¥¢e®­a Bp¡j£ Bqa q®u®­R H¢V Bp¡j£ Bj¡­®L h­®m¢Rm a¡q¡ B¢j ®lLXÑ L¢l</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiNormal; mso-ansi-language: EN;">z</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;"> ...........Bp¡j£ h®­m®­R Cu¡¢LÑ Ll®­a Ll­®a OVe¡¢V O­®V­®Rz l¡¢Lh­®L ¢Q¢Lvp¡l SeÉ i¢aÑ L®­l, Kod ¢L®­e B­®e H¢V h®­m®­Rz l¡¢Lh®­</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiNormal; mso-ansi-language: EN;">L</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;"> j¡l¡l E®­ŸnÉ ¢Rm e¡ H¢V Bp¡j£ h®m®Rz</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; mso-ansi-language: EN;">’ </span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; mso-bidi-font-family: Vrinda; mso-ansi-language: EN;">Pw-38 in cross-examination said,....</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; mso-ansi-language: EN;"> ‘</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;">Bp¡j£ ¢j¾Y¤~ l¡¢Lh­®L ®L¡­®m L®­l q¡pf¡a¡­m ®eu H¢V B¢j ac®­¿¹ ®f®­u¢Rz.........ac®­¿¹ </span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiNormal; mso-ansi-language: EN;">f¡C</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; font-family: MoinaNormal; mso-bidi-font-family: AdarshaLipiExp; mso-ansi-language: EN;">, ¢j¾V¥ l¡¢Lh®­L ®L¡­®m a¥­®m …X ®qmb ¢LÓ¢e­®L ¢e®­u k¡uz</span><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 112%; mso-ansi-language: EN;">’</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 112%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">85.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">From the evidence of aforesaid witnesses it is found that the accused persons removed the victim from the place of occurrence to the hospitals soon after incident. It is also evident by pws-25, 33 and 34 that the accused persons were beaten by angry mobs after occurrence meaning that the accused persons did not flea away rather they tried to save the life of the victim when they felt that they committed serious crime on the victim by pumping air into his belly by inflator. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 112%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">86.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">In such a situation, it is a very hard job for the court to determine the quantum of sentence whether it will be capital punishment or imprisonment for life upon the accused persons since they played a role for saving the victim’s life soon after occurrence as evident by the said prosecution witnesses. At the same time it is very important to note that the victim was completely an innocent teenager who had no fault of such dire consequences at the hands of the accused persons. Since the determination of awarding sentence to the accused persons is at the middle point of views, it may turn to impose capital punishment or imprisonment for life and that is why, the advantage of lesser one shall find the accused persons to acquire in the instant case. More so, both the accused persons have no significant history of prior criminal activities and their PC and PR [previous conviction and previous records] are found nil in the police report. In this regard it finds support from the decision in the case of Nalu –Vs-The State, reported in 1 ALR(AD)(2012) 222 where one of the mitigating factors was previous records of the accused. It also indicates from the evidence of prosecution witnesses that doctors got confused as to how the treatment was given to the victim when he was taken to the hospitals in Khulna Divisional Head Quarters because it was an exceptional offence committed by the accused persons and the victim died around four hours later on the way to Dhaka. Therefore, we do find an extraneous ground to commute the sentences but we do not find any reason to interfere with conviction recorded under sections 302/34 of the Penal Code.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 112%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">87.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">In the above facts and circumstances of the case, we are of the view that ends of justice will be met if the accused persons are sentenced to one of imprisonment for life instead of awarding them sentences to death with a fine of Tk. 50[fifty] thousand each, in default, to under R.I for 02[two] years. On recovery of the fine from both the convicts, the same has to be paid to the legal heirs of the deceased.     </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 112%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">88.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">In the result, the Death Reference No. 92 of 2015 is, hereby, rejected with the said modification in awarding sentences. The Criminal Appeal Nos. 9051 of 2015, 9170 of 2015 and Jail Appeal No. 222 of 2015 and 224 of 2015 are dismissed.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 112%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">89.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Accordingly, both the condemned prisoners are sentenced to imprisonment for life with a fine of Tk. 50[fifty] thousand as stated above and be shifted from the condemned cell to normal cell meant for similar convicts at once. </span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in; line-height: 112%; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 27.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none; margin: 0in 0in 12.0pt 0in;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">90.<span style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal; font-feature-settings: normal; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-synthesis: weight style; font-variant: normal;">        </span></span></strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Let a copy of the judgment and order along with lower court’s records be transmitted to the Metropolitan Sessions Judge, Khulna for taking necessary measures.</span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: .5in; line-height: 112%; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;"><strong><span lang="EN" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 112%;">Ed. </span></strong></span></p><div style="mso-element: footnote-list;"><br clear="all"/><hr align="left" size="1" width="33%"/><div id="ftn1" style="mso-element: footnote;"><p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;
